CodeSystem: Medicamento

Official URL: http://www.saude.gov.br/fhir/r4/CodeSystem/BRMedicamento Version: 0.1.0
Standards status: Informative Maturity Level: 1 Computable Name: BRMedicamento

Drogas dirigidas para uso humano, apresentadas em sua formulação final.

This Code system is referenced in the content logical definition of the following value sets:

  • BRAlergenos

This case-sensitive code system http://www.saude.gov.br/fhir/r4/CodeSystem/BRMedicamento defines the following codes:
